\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ This\ file\ includes\ Linux-\/specific\ support\ functions\ common\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ coredumper\ and\ the\ thread\ lister;\ primarily,\ this\ is\ a\ collection}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ of\ direct\ system\ calls,\ and\ a\ couple\ of\ symbols\ missing\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ standard\ header\ files.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ There\ are\ a\ few\ options\ that\ the\ including\ file\ can\ set\ to\ control}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ behavior\ of\ this\ file:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ SYS\_CPLUSPLUS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ The\ entire\ header\ file\ will\ normally\ be\ wrapped\ in\ 'extern\ "{}C"{}\ \{\ \}"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ making\ it\ suitable\ for\ compilation\ as\ both\ C\ and\ C++\ source.\ If\ you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ do\ not\ want\ to\ do\ this,\ you\ can\ set\ the\ SYS\_CPLUSPLUS\ macro\ to\ inhibit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ the\ wrapping.\ N.B.\ doing\ so\ will\ suppress\ inclusion\ of\ all\ prerequisite}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ system\ header\ files,\ too.\ It\ is\ the\ caller's\ responsibility\ to\ provide}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ the\ necessary\ definitions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ SYS\_ERRNO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ All\ system\ calls\ will\ update\ "{}errno"{}\ unless\ overridden\ by\ setting\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ SYS\_ERRNO\ macro\ prior\ to\ including\ this\ file.\ SYS\_ERRNO\ should\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ an\ l-\/value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ SYS\_INLINE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ New\ symbols\ will\ be\ defined\ "{}static\ inline"{},\ unless\ overridden\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ the\ SYS\_INLINE\ macro.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ SYS\_LINUX\_SYSCALL\_SUPPORT\_H}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ This\ macro\ is\ used\ to\ avoid\ multiple\ inclusions\ of\ this\ header\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ If\ you\ need\ to\ include\ this\ file\ more\ than\ once,\ make\ sure\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ unset\ SYS\_LINUX\_SYSCALL\_SUPPORT\_H\ before\ each\ inclusion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ SYS\_PREFIX:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ New\ system\ calls\ will\ have\ a\ prefix\ of\ "{}sys\_"{}\ unless\ overridden\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ the\ SYS\_PREFIX\ macro.\ Valid\ values\ for\ this\ macro\ are\ [0..9]\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ results\ in\ prefixes\ "{}sys[0..9]\_"{}.\ It\ is\ also\ possible\ to\ set\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ macro\ to\ -\/1,\ which\ avoids\ all\ prefixes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ file\ defines\ a\ few\ internal\ symbols\ that\ all\ start\ with\ "{}LSS\_"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Do\ not\ access\ these\ symbols\ from\ outside\ this\ file.\ They\ are\ not\ part}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ of\ the\ supported\ API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ NOTE:\ This\ is\ a\ stripped\ down\ version\ of\ the\ official\ opensource}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ version\ of\ linux\_syscall\_support.h,\ which\ lives\ at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ http://code.google.com/p/linux-\/syscall-\/support/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ It\ includes\ only\ the\ syscalls\ that\ are\ used\ in\ perftools,\ plus\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ few\ extra.\ \ Here's\ the\ breakdown:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 1)\ Perftools\ uses\ these:\ grep\ -\/rho\ 'sys\_[a-\/z0-\/9\_A-\/Z]*\ *('\ src\ |\ sort\ -\/u}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_\_exit(}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_waitpid(}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 2)\ These\ are\ used\ as\ subroutines\ of\ the\ above:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_getpid\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ gettid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_kill\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ ptrace\_detach}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_restore\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ sigaction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_restore\_rt\ \ \ -\/-\/\ sigaction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_socketcall\ \ \ -\/-\/\ socket}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_wait4\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/\ waitpid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ 3)\ I\ left\ these\ in\ even\ though\ they're\ not\ used.\ \ They\ either}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ complement\ the\ above\ (write\ vs\ read)\ or\ are\ variants\ (rt\_sigaction):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_fstat64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_llseek}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_mmap2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_openat}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ sys\_write}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ SYS\_LINUX\_SYSCALL\_SUPPORT\_H}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00173\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ As\ glibc\ often\ provides\ subtly\ incompatible\ data\ structures\ (and\ implicit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00174\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ wrapper\ functions\ that\ convert\ them),\ we\ provide\ our\ own\ kernel\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00175\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ structures\ for\ use\ by\ the\ system\ calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00176\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ These\ structures\ have\ been\ developed\ by\ using\ Linux\ 2.6.23\ headers\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00177\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ reference.\ Note\ though,\ we\ do\ not\ care\ about\ exact\ API\ compatibility}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00178\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ with\ the\ kernel,\ and\ in\ fact\ the\ kernel\ often\ does\ not\ have\ a\ single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00179\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ API\ that\ works\ across\ architectures.\ Instead,\ we\ try\ to\ mimic\ the\ glibc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00180\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ API\ where\ reasonable,\ and\ only\ guarantee\ ABI\ compatibility\ with\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00181\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ kernel\ headers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00182\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Most\ notably,\ here\ are\ a\ few\ changes\ that\ were\ made\ to\ the\ structures}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00183\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ defined\ by\ kernel\ headers:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00184\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00185\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/\ we\ only\ define\ structures,\ but\ not\ symbolic\ names\ for\ kernel\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00186\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ types.\ For\ the\ latter,\ we\ directly\ use\ the\ native\ C\ datatype}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00187\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ (i.e.\ "{}unsigned"{}\ instead\ of\ "{}mode\_t"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00188\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/\ in\ a\ few\ cases,\ it\ is\ possible\ to\ define\ identical\ structures\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00189\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ both\ 32bit\ (e.g.\ i386)\ and\ 64bit\ (e.g.\ x86-\/64)\ platforms\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00190\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ standardizing\ on\ the\ 64bit\ version\ of\ the\ data\ types.\ In\ particular,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00191\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ this\ means\ that\ we\ use\ "{}unsigned"{}\ where\ the\ 32bit\ headers\ say}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00192\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ "{}unsigned\ long"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00193\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/\ overall,\ we\ try\ to\ minimize\ the\ number\ of\ cases\ where\ we\ need\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00194\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ conditionally\ define\ different\ structures.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/\ the\ "{}struct\ kernel\_sigaction"{}\ class\ of\ structures\ have\ been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ modified\ to\ more\ closely\ mimic\ glibc's\ API\ by\ introducing\ an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ anonymous\ union\ for\ the\ function\ pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/\ a\ small\ number\ of\ field\ names\ had\ to\ have\ an\ underscore\ appended\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ them,\ because\ glibc\ defines\ a\ global\ macro\ by\ the\ same\ name.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00201\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00202\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ include/linux/dirent.h\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00270\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Some\ kernel\ functions\ (e.g.\ sigaction()\ in\ 2.6.23)\ require\ that\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00271\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ exactly\ match\ the\ size\ of\ the\ signal\ set,\ even\ though\ the\ API\ was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00272\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ intended\ to\ be\ extensible.\ We\ define\ our\ own\ KERNEL\_NSIG\ to\ deal\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00273\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00274\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Please\ note\ that\ glibc\ provides\ signals\ [1..\_NSIG-\/1],\ whereas\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00275\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ kernel\ (and\ this\ header)\ provides\ the\ range\ [1..KERNEL\_NSIG].\ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00276\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ actual\ number\ of\ signals\ is\ obviously\ the\ same,\ but\ the\ constants}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00277\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ differ\ by\ one.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00278\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00279\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef\ \_\_mips\_\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00280\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ KERNEL\_NSIG\ 128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00281\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00282\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ KERNEL\_NSIG\ 64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00283\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00284\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00946\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ (e.g.\ in\ order\ to\ implement\ pthread\_atfork,\ and\ to\ make\ calls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00947\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ cancellable),\ which\ means\ we\ cannot\ call\ these\ functions.\ Instead,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01273\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ sign\ extension.\ \ We\ can't\ cast\ pointers\ directly\ because\ those\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01274\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ 32\ bits,\ and\ gcc\ will\ dump\ ugly\ warnings\ about\ casting\ from\ a\ pointer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01275\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ to\ an\ integer\ of\ a\ different\ size.}}
